Linear-A--Unicode-block structured-concept-Mcs
block.U+10600|67072|𐘀..U+1077F|67455|𐝿

McsHitp-creation: {2018-09-15}

overview of U+10600..U+1077F

description::
· Unicode-block-name= Linear-A
· range= U+10600|67072|𐘀..U+1077F|67455|𐝿
· plane= plane.1
· quantity-of-code-points= 384
· quantity-of-chars= 341
· script= Linear A
· The characters in this block can be used to represent the signs found on the undeciphered Phaistos Disc.
[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unicode_character_property#Block]
[ftp://www.unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/]
